msg:I came to Wuhan for a trip and chose this hotel. The transportation is very convenient. It is right next to the subway. I booked a business room and checked in at 8pm. I asked the front desk for alcohol spray and they said it would be delivered to the room, but it was not delivered until I checked out. Then I took the initiative to ask if there was afternoon tea. The front desk said that it was only available in the executive room, but because I stayed for three days, it was given to me. Would it be gone if I didn't ask? Then I saw people's comments that the deluxe room was given to people who stayed for one day. There was no hand-drawn map, and there was no WeChat butler service. I didn't feel that the service was very enthusiastic. The environment was still okay. The room could see a little bit of the Yellow Crane Tower. The breakfast variety was not rich but the taste was good. The waiter's attitude was also good. The drinks and milk in the mini bar in the room were free. There were cherry blossom mung bean cake snacks in the evening. The afternoon tea had porridge, desserts, fruit yogurt, hot dry noodles, etc., which could be eaten as dinner. The comments about check-out said that there were souvenirs, but they were gone when I got here. It might be random! Overall it's ok, more than 600 a night is still cost-effective! One last thing I want to complain about is that the clothesline in the bathroom is installed too high. I wanted to stand on it with a chair but unfortunately the chair couldn't fit in. In the end I had to stand on the trash can upside down to reach it. I've stayed in many hotels but this is the first time I've seen it installed so high.
